## Instruction

It is exam week now, and today is January 16, 2025.  Check the announcements in Canvas for information and compile a list of the remaining final exams I need to take. Please fill in the table `exam_schedule.xlsx` directly under the workspace; the column names have already been provided, do not change the file name after filling in it.  Remove the ‚Äú-x‚Äù suffix from course codes and course names.  Do not include courses that have already ended, that I do not need to attend, or that explicitly state there is no final exam.  The table must list all courses that have not yet ended, that I need to take, and that do not explicitly state there is no final exam. By default, the proctor is the course instructor. If any exam information has not yet been released, mark the cell as TBD. When filling in the table, completely preserve the original table headers.  

## Initial State

### Local Workspace

### Canvas

```python
    'Location': 'TBD',
    'Information Source(Announcement/Email/Message)': 'Announcement',
    'Course Credit': 3
})

# Create DataFrame
df = pd.DataFrame(exam_data)

# Sort by date (TBD exams at the end)
df['sort_date'] = df['Final Date (MM/DD/YYYY)'].apply(lambda x: datetime(2099, 12, 31) if x == 'TBD' else datetime.strptime(x, '%m/%d/%Y'))
df = df.sort_values('sort_date').drop('sort_date', axis=1)

# Save to Excel
df.to_excel('/workspace/dumps/workspace/exam_schedule.xlsx', index=False)

print("Exam schedule created successfully!")
print(f"Total exams: {len(df)}")
print("\nExam Schedule:")
print(df.to_string(index=False)) code
```

```python
import pandas as pd

# Read the created Excel file to verify
df = pd.read_excel('/workspace/dumps/workspace/exam_schedule.xlsx')
print("Final exam schedule verification:")
print(f"File shape: {df.shape}")
print(f"Columns: {list(df.columns)}")
print("\nData:")
print(df.to_string(index=False))

# Check if all courses have "-x" suffix removed
print("\nChecking course codes and names:")
for _, row in df.iterrows():
    course_code = row['Course Code']
    course_name = row['Course Name']
    print(f"{course_code}: {course_name}")
    
    # Verify no "-x" suffix
    if '-x' in course_code.lower() or '-x' in course_name.lower():
        print(f"  WARNING: Found '-x' suffix in {course_code} - {course_name}") code
```

## Summary

I have successfully created the `exam_schedule.xlsx` file with all the remaining final exams you need to take. The file includes:

### **Exams with Confirmed Dates (6 exams):**
1. **CS201 - Data Structures and Algorithms** - Today (Jan 16, 2025) at 9:00 AM, 150 minutes, Building B Room 203
2. **CS302 - Software Engineering Practice** - Jan 17, 2025 at 9:00 AM, 120 minutes, Building C Room 305  
3. **CS401 - Software Engineering** - Jan 17, 2025 at 2:00 PM, 180 minutes, Building C Room 301
4. **AI101 - Fundamentals of Artificial Intelligence** - Jan 18, 2025 at 9:00 AM, 120 minutes, Building A Room 201
5. **MATH101 - Linear Algebra** - Jan 20, 2025 at 2:00 PM, 120 minutes, Building C Room 101
6. **MATH201 - Advanced Mathematics** - Jan 20, 2025 at 9:00 AM, 150 minutes, Building B Room 301 (Open Book)

### **Exams with TBD Information (4 exams):**
- CS301 - Database Systems (proctor changed to Professor Smith)
- DB101 - Database Systems Fundamentals
- ENG101 - English Foundation (90 minutes, Language Lab L101)
- NET101 - Network Programming

### **Key Features of the Schedule:**
- ‚úÖ Removed "-x" suffix from all course codes and names
- ‚úÖ Preserved original table headers exactly as provided
- ‚úÖ Used "Course Instructor" as default proctor (except CS301)
- ‚úÖ Marked missing information as "TBD"
- ‚úÖ Excluded courses that explicitly state no final exam (NLP101)
